Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageOak Hammock contact form

Requesterpool@jpdev.pro
Test date2023/04/23
Score646
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 646, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 12. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

solos: Score 72. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue focusableOperable

WCAG: 2.1.1

Score: 90

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focOp, score 88 (Operable elements that cannot be Tab-focused and vice versa)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 87

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 69 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 17 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 23 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 38

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 36 (Non-underlined adjacent links)
  • Package axe, test link-in-text-block, score 1 (Link is not distinct from surrounding text without reliance on color)

Issue hoverSurprise

WCAG: 1.4.13

Score: 31

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test hover, score 29 (Hovering is mis-indicated or changes content)

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 24

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 22 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 22

  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 2 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
